          <p style="padding-left:5%;max-width:90%;text-align:center;">

   var positionVideoElement = {
     current_state: window.oas_ad.getState(),
     init: function() {
       this.reposition();
       this.transition();
     },
     reposition: function( _state ) {
       var _state = _state || window.oas_ad.getState();
       switch( _state ) {
         case 'tablet':
           $(".column-three").insertBefore(".tiles");
           $(".item22").insertAfter(".column-two .item21");
           break;
         case 'mobile':
           $(".column-three").insertAfter(".column-two");
           $(".column-two .item22").insertAfter(".column-three");
           break;
         default:
           $(".column-one .item21").insertBefore(".column-two .item22");
           $(".column-three").insertAfter(".grid-content");
       }
       this.current_state = _state;
     },
     transition: function() {
       var _this = this;
       $(window).on('resize', function() {
         var _state = window.oas_ad.getState();
         if( _this.current_state === _state ) {
           return;
         } else {
           _this.reposition();
           if ('object' == typeof window.oas_ad) {
               window.oas_ad.buildPostPositions();
           }
         }
       });
     }
   };
   positionVideoElement.init();

              (function($) {
 							$('#newsletter-alert-signup [name="Subscribe"]').on('click',function(){
 								var _this = $('#newsletter-alert-signup'),
 									email = _this.find('input[name="email"]').val(),
 									CSTargetURL = encodeURIComponent(document.location),
 									errEmailExistsMsg = "It looks like you already have an account. <a href='https://home.autonews.com/clickshare/changeServicesAdd.do?CSActivate=true&addAcct.email=" + encodeURIComponent(email) + "&CSTargetURL=" + CSTargetURL + "'>Please visit our newsletter center to update your preferences.</a>";
 								if(email){
 									$("#CSemail").val(email);
 									$("#CSTargetURL").val(CSTargetURL);
 									if($('#signup-promotion-email').is(":checked")){
 										$('input[name^="selection.promote"').val('Y');
 									} else {
 										$('input[name^="selection.promote"').val('N');
 									}
 									$.ajax({
 										url: window.location.protocol + '//' + window.location.host + '/section/cci?template=clickshare-api-ajax',
 										data: {
 											CSOp: 'findAccount',
 											email: email,
 											cci_token: "c49b66abda85cb3bbef5241d70115158a1129f90773ae35a6e9f5179024febfb12839a3dded351ffee4d703826182ca77bd51a6613eba9bb5e2103ca3fa35347",
 											cci_timestamp: "20180621064038"
 										},
 										dataType: 'json',
 										type: 'GET',
 										timeout: 3000
 									}).done(function(account) {
 										if ( +account.errorCode === 0 && account.response ) {
 											$("#errEmailExists").html(errEmailExistsMsg).css({ "padding" : "10px" });
 											return false;
 										}
 										window.location.href = _this.attr('action') + '?' + _this.serialize();
 									}).fail(function(){
 										$("#errEmailExists").html("Your request timed out. Please submit the form again.").css({ "padding" : "10px" });
 										return false;
 									})
 								} else {
 									alert("Please enter your email address first.");
 									return false;
 								}
 								return false;
 							});
 						})(jQuery);

          <script>
           function jt_onBlur(el) {
     if (el.value == '') {
         el.value = el.defaultValue;
     }
 }
 function jt_onFocus(el) {
     if (el.value == el.defaultValue) {
         el.value = '';
     }
 }
 function search_bar_value_jt_onClick() {
 var valueSearch = document.getElementsByName('t730')[0].value;
 if (valueSearch == 'Find Jobs') {
 valueSearch = '';
 }
 window.open('http://jobs.autonews.com/jobseeker/search/?&site_id=2164&t730=' +valueSearch);
 }
          </script>

 $(document).ready(function() {
 	$(".account").click(function() {
 		var X=$(this).attr('id');
 		if(X==1) {
 			$(".submenu").hide();
 			$(this).attr('id', '0');
 		} else {
 			$(".submenu").show();
 			$(this).attr('id', '1');
 		}
 	});
 	//Mouse click on sub menu
 	$(".submenu").mouseup(function() {
 		return false;
 	});
 	//Mouse click on my account link
 	$(".account").mouseup(function() {
 		return false;
 	});
 	//Document Click
 	$(document).mouseup(function() {
 		$(".submenu").hide();
 		$(".account").attr('id', '');
 	});

     function iphoneMenuIssue(){

 	var RemoveTopSpace = function() {
 	    if ($("#oas_x03").find('iframe').length > 0) {
 	    $("body").addClass("pushdown");
 	     $(window).scroll(function(){
                  var lastScroll = 0;
 		 var scroll = $(window).scrollTop();
 		 if (scroll >60) {
 		     $("body").removeClass("pushdown");
 		     } else {
 		     $("body").addClass("pushdown");
 		     }
 	        lastScroll = scroll;
 	    });
 	    }
 	}

 		iphoneMenuIssue();
